SOV_russia_reworked_load_decision_category_russia2 = {
	
	SOV_russia_reworked_load_decision_russia2 = {
		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		visible = {
			has_global_flag = russia_reworked_enabled
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = russia_reworked_loaded
			}
		}
	}
}

	SOV_release_purged_officers = {

		icon = GFX_decision_hol_exchange_intelligence_data

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}
		
		visible = {
			
		}

		available = {
			has_government = communism
			date > 1940.01.01
		}

		cost = 450

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
			    ideology = communism
			    popularity = -0.10
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
			custom_effect_tooltip = result_depending_choice_during_purge_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = purge_1_group_a
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_following_officers
				show_ideas_tooltip = alexander_yegorov
				show_ideas_tooltip = mikhail_frinovsky
				clr_country_flag = purge_1_group_alternative_a
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Nikolai Berzarin"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Nikolai_Berzarin.dds"
					traits = { infantry_officer }
					skill = 3
					
					attack_skill = 3
					defense_skill = 3
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 2
				}
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Alexander Gorbatov"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Alexander_Gorbatov.dds"
					traits = { career_officer cavalry_officer }
					skill = 3
					
					attack_skill = 2
					defense_skill = 3
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = purge_1_group_b
				}
				show_ideas_tooltip = semyon_timoshenko
				show_ideas_tooltip = konstantin_rokossovsky
				show_ideas_tooltip = ivan_yumashev
				clr_country_flag = purge_1_group_alternative_b

					name = "Konstantin Rokossovsky"

					attack_skill = 3
					defense_skill = 4
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 4
				}
				create_corps_commander = {
					name = "Semyon Timoshenko"
					picture = "Portrait_Soviet_Semyon_Timoshenko.dds"
					traits = { cavalry_officer politically_connected career_officer }
					skill = 3
					
					attack_skill = 3
					defense_skill = 2
					planning_skill = 2
					logistics_skill = 3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = purge_2_group_a
				}
				show_ideas_tooltip = pavel_rychagov
				show_ideas_tooltip = gordey_levchenko

SOV_move_capital_neutrality = {

	SOV_move_capital_195 = {

		icon = GFX_decision_infiltrate_state

		fire_only_once = yes

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}
		
		visible = {
			has_government = neutrality
			has_country_flag = second_civil_war_over
		}

		available = {
			has_government = neutrality
			has_full_control_of_state = 195
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = move_capital_is_not_195
				any_state = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_capital = yes
					NOT = {
						state = 195
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 25

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_war = yes
				surrender_progress > 0.25
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = FIN
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.236 }
		}
	}
}

SOV_europe_expansion = {

    SOV_join_the_war_against_poland = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_tank

     	available = {
			date > 1939.09.17
			has_idea = SOV_molotov_ribbentrop_pact
			POL = {
				exists = yes
				has_war_with = GER
				NOT = {
					has_capitulated = yes
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					has_capitulated = yes
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					NOT = {
						tag = POL
					}
					is_major = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_in_faction_with = POL
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_neighbor_of = POL
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
					is_neighbor_of = POL
				}
			}
     	}

		visible = {
			POL = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		target_root_trigger = {
			tag = SOV
			has_completed_focus = SOV_russian_expansion
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = POL
			}
		}

     	fire_only_once = yes

     	cost = 50

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 2000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					any_other_country = {
						is_major = yes
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = POL
							has_guaranteed = POL
						}
					}
					POL = {
						has_idea = anti_soviet_pact
					}
				}
			}
		}

     	complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = sov_russian_expansion_war_poland
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_guaranteed = POL
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = POL
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = POL
					type = take_state_focus
					generator = { 89 91 93 94 95 96 784 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

    SOV_demand_poland = {

		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support

     	available = {
     	    has_army_manpower = {
    			size > 1500000
    		}
			NOT = {
				has_idea = SOV_molotov_ribbentrop_pact
			}
			POL = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_neighbor_of = POL
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
					is_neighbor_of = POL
				}
			}
     	}

		visible = {
			POL = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		target_root_trigger = {
			tag = SOV
			has_completed_focus = SOV_russian_expansion
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = POL
			}
		}

     	fire_only_once = yes

     	cost = 100

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 2000
			modifier = {
				GER = {
					has_war_with = POL
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}

     	complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = sov_russian_expansion_ultimatum_poland
			if = {
				limit = {
					POL = {
						is_subject = yes
					}
				}
				POL = {
					OVERLORD = {
						country_event = { hours = 6 id = polands.1 }
						custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_demand_poland_tt
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				POL = {
					country_event = { hours = 6 id = polands.1 }
				}
			}
		}
    }

    SOV_demand_bessarabia = {

		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support

     	available = {
     	    has_army_manpower = {
    			size > 1000000
    		}
			78 = {
				OWNER = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 78
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					is_neighbor_of = ROOT
				}
			}

					has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_2
					has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_3
					has_idea = SOV_Supporters_fourth_international
					has_idea = SOV_Fight_revolution
				}
			}
		}

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_communist_minorities_europe
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				has_government = communism
				NOT = { 
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_civil_war = yes 
				}
				is_major = no
				NOT = {
					TAG = SLV
					TAG = CRO
					TAG = BOS
					TAG = SER
					TAG = MNT
					TAG = MAC
					TAG = CAT
					TAG = NAV
					TAG = GLC

					TAG = WLS
					TAG = NIR
					tag = KOR
					tag = VIN
					tag = CAM
					tag = LAO
					tag = TIB
					tag = ETH
					tag = MOR
					tag = EGY
					has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_1
					has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_2
					has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_3
					has_idea = SOV_Supporters_fourth_international
					has_idea = SOV_Fight_revolution
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 29
				}
				FROM = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = ROOT
						value > 29
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				is_subject = no
				is_faction_leader = no
				OR = {
					has_government = communism
					communism > 0.4
				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = soviets.69
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

SOV_invite_revolution = {

	SOV_invite_communist_revolution = {

		icon = GFX_generic_political_discourse

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 10

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		visible = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_completed_focus = SOV_revolution_to_the_utmost
			any_country = {
				has_country_flag = liberated_by_sov
			}
			has_government = communism
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				has_government = communism
				has_country_flag = liberated_by_sov
			}
		}

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_revolution_to_the_utmost
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				has_government = communism
				has_country_flag = liberated_by_sov
			}
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 49
				}
				FROM = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = ROOT
						value > 49
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				is_subject = no
				has_government = communism
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
				NOT = {
					has_idea = SOV_Fight_revolution
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 10

		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = soviets.98
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

	SOV_expand_revolution = {

		icon = generic_industry

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 50

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_consolidate_true_communism
		}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_expand_revolution_tt
				has_country_flag = SOV_secured_revolution
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_expand_revolution_tt2
				has_country_flag = SOV_has_conquered_major_city_europe
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_expand_revolution_tt3
				check_variable = {
					var = revolution_count
					value = 6
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SOV_Marching_revolution
				add_idea = SOV_Marching_revolution2
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_tech = tech_logistics_company
						}
					}
					set_technology = {
						tech_logistics_company = 1
					}
				}
				if = {

						}

					}
					set_state_flag = give_back_mil_after_air_raid

				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_reform_entente
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				OR = {
					tag = ENG
					tag = USA
					tag = ITA
					tag = SER
					tag = MNT
					tag = BEL
					tag = SAU
					tag = POR
					tag = ROM
					tag = GRE
					tag = SIA
					tag = BRA
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 49
				}
				FROM = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = ROOT
						value > 49
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				is_subject = no
				OR = {
					has_government = democratic
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							tag = USA
						}
					}

					has_war_support > 0.5
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_country_flag = is_target_of_SOV_democratic
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = is_target_of_SOV_democratic
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						tag = ENG
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					ENG = {
						has_country_flag = cut_all_diplomatic_ties_with_sov
					}
					has_idea = SOV_Blockaded_by_eng
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = soviets.154
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

SOV_perpetual_defense_liberty_decisions = {

	SOV_demand_change_government = {

		icon = GFX_decision_hol_war_on_pacifism

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 30

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		visible = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_government = democratic
							}
						}
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_capitulated = yes
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_capitulated = yes
					has_government = democratic
					tag = POL
					tag = LIT
					tag = LAT
					tag = EST
					tag = ROM
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = FROM
					is_capital = yes
				}
			}
		}

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_perpetual_defense_liberty
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					is_neighbor_of = ROOT
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_neighbor_of = FROM
					}
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						is_neighbor_of = FROM
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_capitulated = yes
					has_government = democratic
					tag = POL
					tag = LIT
					tag = LAT
					tag = EST
					tag = ROM
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = FROM
					is_capital = yes
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = FROM
			is_capital = yes
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = is_changing_foreign_government
			}
			FROM = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = is_changing_foreign_government
			FROM = {
				country_event = soviets.331
				set_country_flag = is_target_of_SOV_democratic
				activate_mission = SOV_is_building_up_against_from_democratic
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = soviets.170
				}
				clr_country_flag = is_target_of_SOV_democratic
			}
			clr_country_flag = is_changing_foreign_government
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				add = -90
				has_war = yes
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = FROM
					}
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						has_guaranteed = FROM
					}
					FROM = {
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					alliance_strength_ratio > 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	SOV_send_recon_team_central_russia = {

		}

	SOV_send_recon_team_transvolga_region = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_intelligence_operation

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		available = {
			command_power > 15
		}

		visible = {
			has_idea = SOV_Communist_resistance3
			has_country_flag = transvolga_region_claims
			has_completed_focus = SOV_destroy_communist
		}

		highlight_state_targets = {
			state = 399
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 15
		}

		cost = 0

		days_remove = 25

		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
						    var = recon_team_transvolga_region_variables
						    value = 75
						    compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
					SOV = {
						country_event = { id = soviets.202 hours = 2 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					SOV = {
						country_event = { id = soviets.243 hours = 2 }
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = recon_team_transvolga_region_variables
						value = 20
					}
					randomize_variable = {
						var = recon_team_transvolga_region_variables
						distribution = uniform
						min = recon_team_transvolga_region_variables
						max = 100
					}
					round_variable = recon_team_transvolga_region_variables
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_send_recon_team_transvolga_region_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -15
			}
		}
	}

			has_completed_focus = SOV_russianize_the_balkans
			HUN = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_russianize_the_balkans
		}

		cost = 150

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 150
		}

		days_remove = 140

		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.15
			industrial_capacity_factory = -0.25
			research_speed_factor = -0.15
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = is_russianizing_a_country
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = SOV_Russianization_balkan_large
			}
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = {
				HUN = {
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
		}

		cancel_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = is_russianizing_a_country
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = SOV_Russianization_balkan_large
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = SOV_Russianization_balkan_large
			}
			clr_country_flag = is_russianizing_a_country
			custom_effect_tooltip = gain_between_20_and_30_russianization_hungary
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = russianization_hungary_gain
				value = 20
			}
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = russianization_hungary_gain
				distribution = uniform
				min = russianization_hungary_gain
				max = 30
			}
			round_temp_variable = russianization_hungary_gain
			add_to_variable = {
				var = hungary_russianization_slavic
				value = russianization_hungary_gain
			}
		}
	}

	SOV_russianize_hungary_decision_slavic = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_nationalism

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		available = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_russianize_the_balkans

				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}

SOV_defend_slavic_borders_category = {

	SOV_fortify_slavic_border_states = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_construction

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		state_target = yes

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_core_of = SOV
				any_neighbor_state = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = SOV
						is_fully_controlled_by = SOV
					}
				}
				bunker < 7
				anti_air_building < 4
			}
		}

		available = {
			ROOT = {
				has_full_control_of_state = FROM
			}
			FROM = {
				bunker < 7
				anti_air_building < 4
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = fortification_slavic_country_timeout
			}
		}

		visible = {
			FROM = {
				is_core_of = SOV
				any_neighbor_state = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = SOV
						is_fully_controlled_by = SOV
					}
				}
				bunker < 7
				anti_air_building < 4
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 50

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 150
		}

		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 10
		}

		days_remove = 70

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = fortification_slavic_country_timeout
		}

		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = fortification_slavic_country_timeout
			FROM = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = bunker
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
					province = {
						all_provinces = yes
						limit_to_border = yes
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = anti_air_building
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						NOT = {
							infrastructure > 7
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 3
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

							traits = { career_officer }
							skill = 1
							attack_skill = 1
							defense_skill = 1
							planning_skill = 1
							logistics_skill = 1
						}
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = soviets.207 }
					country_event = { id = soviets.208 }
					country_event = { id = soviets.209 }
				}
			}

SOV_monarchy_congress = {

	#Have to do each house one by one because Paradox doesn't allow the use of a foreach here
	SOV_monarchy_support_house_1 = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = less_than_3_house_1
				check_variable = {
					var = house_russia^1
					value = 3
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = is_supporting_house
			}
		}

		cost = house_russia_pp_cost^1

		days_remove = house_russia_pp_cost^1

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = is_supporting_house
		}

		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = is_supporting_house
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_monarchy_support_house_1_tt

			add_to_variable = {
				var = house_russia^1
				value = 1
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = house_russia^1
						value = 2
						compare = equals
					}
				}
				set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^1 = 20 }
				add_to_variable = {
					var = house_russia_neutral
					value = 1
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = house_russia_opposed
					value = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = house_russia^1
						value = 3
						compare = equals
					}
				}
				set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^1 = 10 }
				add_to_variable = {
					var = house_russia_support
					value = 1
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = house_russia_neutral
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	SOV_monarchy_support_house_2 = {

					value = 3
					compare = less_than
				}
			}

				has_country_flag = is_supporting_house
			}
		}

		cost = house_russia_pp_cost^2

		days_remove = house_russia_pp_cost^2

			set_country_flag = is_supporting_house
		}

		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = is_supporting_house
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_monarchy_support_house_2_tt

			add_to_variable = {
				var = house_russia^2
				value = 1
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = house_russia^2
						value = 2
						compare = equals
					}
				}
				set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^2 = 20 }
				add_to_variable = {
					var = house_russia_neutral
					value = 1
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = house_russia_opposed
					value = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = house_russia^2
						value = 3
						compare = equals
					}
				}
				set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^2 = 10 }
				add_to_variable = {
					var = house_russia_support
					value = 1
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = house_russia_neutral
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}

	SOV_coalition_party = {

		icon = GFX_decision_hol_exchange_intelligence_data

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_coalition_party_tt
				check_variable = {
					var = house_russia_opposed
					value = 1
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = is_supporting_house
			}
		}

		cost = 60

		days_remove = 30

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = is_supporting_house
		}

		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = is_supporting_house
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_1_house_go_support

			set_temp_variable = { success_count = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { random_count_array = 0 }
			while_loop_effect = {
				break = end_array
    			limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = success_count
						value = 1
						compare = less_than
					}
				}

				for_each_loop = {
				    array = monarchy_houses_russia
					value = current
	    			index = i
				    break = end_array

				    if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = {
								var = house_russia^var:current
								value = 1
								compare = equals
							}
						}
						randomize_temp_variable = {
							var = random_count_array
							distribution = uniform
							min = 1
							max = 2
						}
						round_temp_variable = random_count_array
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = random_count_array
									value = 1
									compare = equals
								}
							}
							set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^var:current = 10 }
							add_to_variable = {
								var = house_russia_support
								value = 1
							}
							subtract_from_variable = {
								var = house_russia_opposed
								value = 1
							}
							add_to_variable = {
								var = house_russia^var:current
								value = 2
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { success_count = 1 }
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = {
										var = success_count
										value = 1
										compare = equals
									}
								}
								add_to_temp_variable = { end_array = 1 }
							}
						}
						else = {
							# Nothing happens, the loop will keep going
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	SOV_war_economy_law_parl = {

		icon = GFX_decision_ger_military_buildup

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = war_economy
					has_idea = tot_economic_mobilisation
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_war = yes
				AND = {
					has_war_support > 0.5
					threat > 0.5
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_war_economy_law_parl_support_tt
				check_variable = {
					var = house_russia_support
					value = 6
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_war_economy_law_parl_opposition_tt
				check_variable = {
					var = house_russia_opposed
					value = 2
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		complete_effect = {
			add_ideas = war_economy
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_2_houses_go_opposition

			set_temp_variable = { success_count = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { random_count_array = 0 }
			while_loop_effect = {
				break = end_array
    			limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = success_count
						value = 2
						compare = less_than
					}
				}

				for_each_loop = {
				    array = monarchy_houses_russia
					value = current
	    			index = i
				    break = end_array

				    if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = {
								var = house_russia^var:current
								value = 3
								compare = equals
							}
						}
						randomize_temp_variable = {
							var = random_count_array
							distribution = uniform
							min = 1
							max = 2
						}
						round_temp_variable = random_count_array
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = random_count_array
									value = 1
									compare = equals
								}
							}
							set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^var:current = 30 }
							add_to_variable = {
								var = house_russia_opposed
								value = 1
							}
							subtract_from_variable = {
								var = house_russia_support
								value = 1
							}
							subtract_from_variable = {
								var = house_russia^var:current
								value = 2
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { success_count = 1 }
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = {
										var = success_count
										value = 2
										compare = equals
									}
								}
								add_to_temp_variable = { end_array = 1 }
							}
						}
						else = {
							# Nothing happens, the loop will keep going
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	SOV_increase_ressources_law_parl = {

		icon = GFX_decision_tungsten
		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		available = {
			owns_state = 219
			owns_state = 232
			owns_state = 233
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_increase_ressources_law_parl_support_tt
				check_variable = {
					var = house_russia_support
					value = 4
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = SOV_increase_ressources_law_parl_opposition_tt
				check_variable = {
					var = house_russia_opposed
					value = 3
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		complete_effect = {
			add_ideas = SOV_Develop_new_ressources
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_Payment_ressources
				days = 180
			}
			219 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = rubber
					amount = 10
				}
			}
			232 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = oil
					amount = 10
				}
			}
			233 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = tungsten
					amount = 16
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_2_houses_go_opposition
			set_temp_variable = { success_count = 0 }
			set_temp_variable = { random_count_array = 0 }
			while_loop_effect = {
				break = end_array
    			limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = success_count
						value = 2
						compare = less_than
					}
				}

				for_each_loop = {
				    array = monarchy_houses_russia
					value = current
	    			index = i
				    break = end_array

				    if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = {
								var = house_russia^var:current
								value = 3
								compare = equals
							}
						}
						randomize_temp_variable = {
							var = random_count_array
							distribution = uniform
							min = 1
							max = 2
						}
						round_temp_variable = random_count_array
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									var = random_count_array
									value = 1
									compare = equals
								}
							}
							set_variable = { house_russia_pp_cost^var:current = 30 }
							add_to_variable = {
								var = house_russia_opposed
								value = 1
							}
							subtract_from_variable = {
								var = house_russia_support
								value = 1
							}
							subtract_from_variable = {
								var = house_russia^var:current
								value = 2
							}
							add_to_temp_variable = { success_count = 1 }
							if = {
								limit = {
									check_variable = {
										var = success_count
										value = 2
										compare = equals
									}
								}
								add_to_temp_variable = { end_array = 1 }
							}
						}
						else = {
							# Nothing happens, the loop will keep going
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

SOV_reintegrate_lost_states_decisions = {

	SOV_integrate_ukraine = { #Version if you didn't sympathized with the Ukrainian and if they for some reasons agree

		icon = GFX_decision_infiltrate_state

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		available = {
			UKR = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
			}
			UKR = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			country_exists = UKR
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 75

		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { stability_calculator_ukraine_1 = stability_hit_ukraine }
			multiply_temp_variable = { stability_calculator_ukraine_1 = 0.05 }
			set_temp_variable = { army_transfer_calculator_ukr = army_transfer_ukr_lost }
			multiply_temp_variable = { army_transfer_calculator_ukr = 0.2 }
			set_temp_variable = { army_transfer_calculator_ukr_tt = army_transfer_calculator_ukr }
			multiply_temp_variable = { army_transfer_calculator_ukr_tt = 100 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = transfer_ukr_army_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				UKR = {
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = SOV
						size = army_transfer_calculator_ukr
						army_ratio = army_transfer_calculator_ukr
						stockpile_ratio = army_transfer_calculator_ukr
					}
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				annex_country = {
					target = UKR
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							check_variable = {
								var = stability_calculator_ukraine_1
								value = 0
								compare = equals
							}
						}
					}
					add_stability = stability_calculator_ukraine_1
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = soviets.219 hours = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	SOV_integrate_ukraine_2 = { #Version if you did sympathized with the Ukrainian

		icon = GFX_decision_infiltrate_state

					}

			SOV = {
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = soviets.219 hours = 1 }
				}
				clr_country_flag = ukraine_no_imperial_govern
			}
		}
	}

	SOV_reinforce_imperial_ties_ukraine = {

		icon = GFX_decision_eng_ally_imperialist_coup

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = reinforce_imperial_ties_ukraine_tt
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = stability_hit_ukraine
							value = 3
							compare = equals
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = reinforce_imperial_ties_ukraine_tt2
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = stability_hit_ukraine
							value = 3
							compare = equals
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			UKR = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
		}

		cost = 25

		days_remove = 30

		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { stability_calculator_ukraine_1 = stability_hit_ukraine }
			multiply_temp_variable = { stability_calculator_ukraine_1 = -5 }
			set_temp_variable = { stability_calculator_ukraine_2 = stability_hit_ukraine }
			multiply_temp_variable = { stability_calculator_ukraine_2 = -5 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = stability_ukr_upgrade_tt
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = stability_ukr_upgrade_original_tt
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = stability_hit_ukraine
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

	SOV_army_integration_ukraine = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_army_support

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = sympathize_with_ukraine
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SOV_army_integration_ukraine1_tt
					check_variable = {
						var = stability_hit_ukraine
						value = 0
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SOV_army_integration_ukraine2_tt
					check_variable = {
						var = stability_hit_ukraine
						value = 0
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = army_transfer_ukr_lost_tt
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						var = army_transfer_ukr_lost
						value = 5
						compare = equals
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			UKR = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
		}

		cost = 25

		days_remove = 40

		remove_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { army_transfer_calculator_ukr = army_transfer_ukr_lost }
			multiply_temp_variable = { army_transfer_calculator_ukr = 20 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = army_transfer_calculator_ukr
						value = 100
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = { army_transfer_calculator_ukr = 20 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = army_integration_ukr_absorb_tt
			add_to_variable = {
				var = army_transfer_ukr_lost

			FROM = {

					has_country_flag = germany_no_imperial_transform
				}
			}

		}

					target = FROM

	form_oceania_russia_continent = {

		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support

		available = {
			any_state = {
				has_state_flag = oceania_fascist_nation_puppet
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			is_subject = no
		}


		fire_only_once = yes

	   ai_will_do = {
		   factor = 100
	   }

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = form_oceania_continent_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = oceania_fascist_nation_puppet
						NOT = {
							is_claimed_by = SOV
							is_core_of = SOV
						}
					}
					OCE = {
						add_state_core = PREV
					}	
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = SOV_Impose_order
					}
					release_autonomy = {
						target = OCE
						autonomy_state = autonomy_state_magistrate
					}
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 10
						neutrality = 10
						fascism = 70
						communism = 10
					}
				}
				else = {
					SOV = {
						release_autonomy = {
							target = OCE
							autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate
							freedom_level = 0.5
						}
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 10
							neutrality = 10
							fascism = 70
							communism = 10
						}
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = oceania_fascist_nation_puppet
						is_claimed_by = SOV
					}
					OCE = {
						add_state_core = PREV
					}	
				}
				OCE = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							SOV = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Konstantin Rodzaevsky"
								}
							}
						}
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Administrative Department of Oceania"
							desc = "POLITICS_ADMIN_DEPT_DESC"
							picture = "Provisional_Government_Fascism.dds"
							expire = "1953.3.1"
							ideology = fascism_ideology
							traits = {
									
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							SOV = {
								has_idea = SOV_Impose_order
							}	
						}
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "State Magistrate of Oceania"
							desc = "POLITICS_STATE_MAGISTRATE_DESC"
							picture = "Provisional_Government_Fascism.dds"
							expire = "1953.3.1"
							ideology = fascism_ideology
							traits = {
									
							}
						}
					}
					inherit_technology = SOV
					division_template = {
						name = "Island Garrison Division"
						priority = 1
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 4 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 4 }
						}
						support = {
							engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							artillery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
					}
					random_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"1st Island Garrison Division\" division_template = \"Island Garrison Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"

			NAF = {

			}
		}

		visible = {
			NAF = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			any_state = {

					has_state_flag = north_america_fascist_nation_puppet

SOV_focus_fascist_russia_europe = {

	SOV_bonus_against_from_europe = {

		icon = GFX_decision_hol_war_on_pacifism

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SOV_fascist_focus_on_europe
		}

		highlight_states = {
			is_controlled_by = FROM
			is_capital = yes
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				capital_scope = {
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				OR = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						is_justifying_wargoal_against = ROOT
						has_wargoal_against = ROOT
						is_neighbor_of = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							is_justifying_wargoal_against = FROM
							has_wargoal_against = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				capital_scope = {
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				OR = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						is_justifying_wargoal_against = ROOT
						has_wargoal_against = ROOT
						is_neighbor_of = ROOT
					}
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							is_justifying_wargoal_against = FROM
							has_wargoal_against = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			FROM = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}

		cost = 10

		days_remove = 100

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		targeted_modifier = {
			tag = FROM
			attack_bonus_against = 0.1
			defense_bonus_against = 0.1
		}
	}
}

SOV_expand_russian_dominance = {

	SOV_demande_border_state = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_tank

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		target_array = neighbors

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_new_russian_era
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_neighbor_of = ROOT
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					is_subject = yes
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_capitulated = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = FROM
					is_capital = yes
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			FROM = {
				is_neighbor_of = ROOT
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					is_subject = yes
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_capitulated = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = FROM
					is_capital = yes
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = FROM
			is_capital = yes
		}

		available = {
			is_major = yes
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = is_building_up_border_fascist
			}
			NOT = {
				FROM = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = {
								has_idea = SOV_Closed_alliance
							}
						}
						has_country_flag = SOV_is_demanding_alliance
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				add = -90
				has_war = yes
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						is_in_faction_with = FROM
					}
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						has_guaranteed = FROM
					}
					FROM = {
						is_major = yes
					}
				}

SOV_invite_neighbours = {

	SOV_demande_alliance = {

		icon = GFX_decision_hol_exchange_intelligence_data

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		target_array = neighbors #Doesn't seem to work that well so we add is_neighbor_of as well

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_idea = SOV_Closed_alliance
		}

		visible = {
			is_subject = no
			has_government = fascism
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_idea = SOV_Closed_alliance
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_major = yes
					is_subject = yes
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				is_neighbor_of = ROOT
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					is_major = yes
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_capitulated = yes
					is_subject = yes
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = FROM
					is_capital = yes
				}
				capital_scope = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
				}
			}
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_neighbor_of = ROOT
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					is_major = yes
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_capitulated = yes
					is_subject = yes
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = FROM
					is_capital = yes
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = FROM
			is_capital = yes
		}

		available = {
			is_major = yes
			NOT = {
				FROM = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					if = {
						limit = {
							ROOT = {
								has_completed_focus = SOV_new_russian_era
							}
						}
						has_country_flag = is_target_of_SOV_fascist
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = soviets.353
				set_country_flag = SOV_is_demanding_alliance
			}
		}
	}
}

SOV_communist_influence_international = {

	SOV_end_communist_threat = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_independence

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			OR = {
				has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_1
				has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_2
				has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_3
			}
        }

        available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = communist_party_threat_big_enough
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = communist_influence_2_ready
						days > 100
					}
					communism > 0.2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_1
				}
				communism < 0.05
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_2
				}
				communism < 0.15
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Communist_influence_international_3
				}

					var = pocket_penalty_black_guard
					value = -0.8
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 25

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_survivalist_black_guard_variable_tt
			add_to_variable = { pocket_penalty_black_guard = -0.10 }
			set_variable = { loca_pocket_penalty_black_guard = pocket_penalty_black_guard }
			multiply_variable = { loca_pocket_penalty_black_guard = 100.00 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_army_vigilance_2_5
			add_to_variable = {
				var = army_vigiliance_black_revolution
				value = 2.5
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}

		}

					remove_ideas = home_of_revolution
					add_ideas = extensive_conscription
					add_ideas = SOV_Determination
					add_ideas = SOV_Surprise_attack_black_revolution
					country_event = { id = soviets.404 hours = 1 }
					country_event = { id = soviets.405 hours = 1 }
					country_event = { id = soviets.406 hours = 2 }
					country_event = { id = soviets.407 hours = 2 }
					country_event = { id = soviets.408 hours = 1 }
					country_event = { id = soviets.411 hours = 2 }
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Strelkovaya Diviziya"
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Gornostrelkovaya Diviziya"
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Motostrelkovaya Diviziya"
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Kavaleriyskaya Diviziya"
					}

						division_template = "NKVD Pogranichnaya Diviziya"

						division_template = "Mekhanizirovaniy Korpus"
					}
					dismantle_faction = yes
					retire_ideology_leader = communism
					destroy_ships = {
						type = destroyer
						count = all
					}
					destroy_ships = {

						count = all
					}
					destroy_ships = {
						type = ship_hull_submarine_2
						count = all

						type = ship_hull_heavy_1
						count = all

					destroy_ships = {
						type = light_cruiser

					}
					destroy_ships = {

						count = all
					}
					destroy_ships = {
						type = battleship_1
						count = all
					}
					destroy_ships = {

					}

						retire = yes
					}
				}
				SOU = {

						type = annex_everything

SOV_crush_the_anti_revolutionary = {
	
	SOV_recon_the_area = {
	
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		state_target = yes

		target_array = SOV.sov_recon_rebel_anarchy_states

		visible = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					has_state_flag = recon_units_scout_place
				}
			}
			PREV = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = found_small_base_1
						has_country_flag = found_small_base_2
						has_country_flag = found_small_base_3
						has_country_flag = found_medium_base_1
						has_country_flag = found_medium_base_2
						has_country_flag = found_large_base
					}	
				}
			}
				
		}

		days_remove = 7

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 10

		available = {
			NOT = {
				PREV = {
					has_country_flag = doing_recon_area
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				set_state_flag = recon_units_scout_place
			}
			PREV = {
				set_country_flag = doing_recon_area
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_recon_the_area_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_state_flag = small_counter_revolution_resistance_1
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					save_event_target_as = SOV_successful_recon_small
					set_state_flag = found_small_counter_revolution_base_1
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					PREV = {
						country_event = { id = soviets.416 }
						set_country_flag = found_small_base_1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_state_flag = small_counter_revolution_resistance_2
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					save_event_target_as = SOV_successful_recon_small
					set_state_flag = found_small_counter_revolution_base_2
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					PREV = {
						country_event = { id = soviets.416 }
						set_country_flag = found_small_base_2
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_state_flag = small_counter_revolution_resistance_3
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					save_event_target_as = SOV_successful_recon_small
					set_state_flag = found_small_counter_revolution_base_3
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					PREV = {
						country_event = { id = soviets.416 }
						set_country_flag = found_small_base_3
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_state_flag = medium_counter_revolution_resistance_1
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					save_event_target_as = SOV_successful_recon_medium
					set_state_flag = found_medium_counter_revolution_base_1
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					PREV = {
						country_event = { id = soviets.417 }
						set_country_flag = found_medium_base_1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_state_flag = medium_counter_revolution_resistance_2
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					save_event_target_as = SOV_successful_recon_medium
					set_state_flag = found_medium_counter_revolution_base_2
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					PREV = {
						country_event = { id = soviets.417 }
						set_country_flag = found_medium_base_2
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						has_state_flag = large_counter_revolution_resistance_1
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					save_event_target_as = SOV_successful_recon_large
					set_state_flag = found_large_counter_revolution_base
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					PREV = {
						country_event = { id = soviets.418 }
						set_country_flag = found_large_base
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {

		days_mission_timeout = 60

		is_good = no

		timeout_effect = {
			SOV = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -1000
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = -50
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = artillery_equipment
					amount = -25
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = light_tank_equipment
					amount = -25
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = motorized_equipment
					amount = -75
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						non_damaged_building_level = {
							building = industrial_complex level > 0
						}
					}
					damage_building = {
						type = industrial_complex damage = 1
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						non_damaged_building_level = {
							building = arms_factory level > 0
						}
					}
					damage_building = {
						type = arms_factory damage = 1
					}
				}
				random_owned_controlled_state = {
					limit = {
						non_damaged_building_level = {
							building = infrastructure level > 1
						}
					}
					damage_building = {
						type = infrastructure
						damage = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {

		}
	}

SOV_track_stalin_decision = {

	SOV_search_for_stalin = {
	
		icon = GFX_decision_infiltrate_state

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		state_target = yes

		target_array = global.sov_track_available_states

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_the_track
			has_government = democratic
			has_country_flag = sov_track_begin
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = sov_stalin_track_found
			}
		}

		days_remove = 10

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 10

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = is_searching_for_stalin
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = is_searching_for_stalin
		}

		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = is_searching_for_stalin
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							has_state_flag = sov_stalin_hidding_state
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = sov_stalin_track_found
					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = {
								CONTROLLER = {
									tag = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
						ROOT = {
							country_event = { id = soviets.434 }
						}
					}
					else = {
						FROM = {
							clr_state_flag = sov_stalin_hidding_state
							set_state_flag = sov_stalin_found_state
							state_event = { id = soviets.432 trigger_for = ROOT }
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						save_event_target_as = stalin_hiding_state_target
					}
					remove_from_array = { global.sov_track_available_states = FROM }
				}
				else = {
					FROM = {
						state_event = { id = soviets.444 trigger_for = ROOT }
					}
					remove_from_array = { global.sov_track_available_states = FROM }
				}
			}
        }

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}	
	}
}

							var = investment_broken_market_vari
							value = 4
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = SOV_Reconstructed_economy
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = investment_broken_market_vari
						value = 4
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = investment_broken_market_vari
							value = 7
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = SOV_Reconstructed_economy_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = investment_broken_market_vari
						value = 7
						compare = equals
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = investment_broken_market_vari
							value = 6
							compare = less_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = SOV_Reconstructed_economy_3
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 60
		}
	}
}

SOV_rename_soviet_cities = {

	SOV_rename_stalingrad = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_decision

		visible = {
			OR = {
				owns_state = 217
				controls_state = 217
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = SOV_stalingrad_renamed
					has_global_flag = SOV_stalingrad_renamed_tsar
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Kirill Vladimirovich"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Vladimir Kirillovich"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Anastasia Nikolaevna"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = SOV_stalingrad_renamed_tsar
					}
				}
				else = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = SOV_stalingrad_renamed
					}
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			state = 217
		}

		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 217
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
					}
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Kirill Vladimirovich"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Vladimir Kirillovich"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Anastasia Nikolaevna"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				set_province_name = { id = 3529 name = "Tsaritsyn"}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_global_flag = SOV_stalingrad_renamed_tsar
					217 = {
						set_state_name = "Tsaritsyn"
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				set_province_name = { id = 3529 name = "Volgograd"}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_global_flag = SOV_stalingrad_renamed
					217 = {
						set_state_name = "Volgograd"
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				reset_province_name = 3529
				hidden_effect = {
					clr_global_flag = SOV_stalingrad_renamed
					clr_global_flag = SOV_stalingrad_renamed_tsar
					217 = {
						reset_state_name = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

					}

				else = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = SOV_leningrad_renamed
					}
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			state = 195
		}

		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 195
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
					}
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Alexander Fyodorovich Kerensky"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Ivan Nikolaevich"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Volin Eikhenbaum"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Peter Arshinov"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Alexei Borovoi"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				set_province_name = { id = 3151 name = "Petrograd"}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_global_flag = SOV_leningrad_renamed_petrograd
					195 = {
						set_state_name = "Petrograd"
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				set_province_name = { id = 3151 name = "Saint Petersburg"}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_global_flag = SOV_leningrad_renamed
					195 = {
						set_state_name = "Saint Petersburg"
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				reset_province_name = 3151
				hidden_effect = {
					clr_global_flag = SOV_leningrad_renamed
					clr_global_flag = SOV_leningrad_renamed_petrograd
					195 = {
						reset_state_name = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

	SOV_relocate_industry_from_moscow_russia2 = {

		icon = generic_construction

		highlight_state_targets = {
			state = 219
		}

		available = {
			219 = { #Moscow
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
				arms_factory > 5
				industrial_complex > 1
			}
			573 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV } #Zlatoust
			582 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV } #Magnitogorsk
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 25

		days_remove = 15

		modifier = {

		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 200 # oh shit they are getting close!
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owns_state = 246
						NOT = { controls_state = 246 }
					}
					AND = {
						owns_state = 242
						NOT = { controls_state = 242 }
					}
					AND = {
						owns_state = 205
						NOT = { controls_state = 205 }
					}
					AND = {
						owns_state = 223
						NOT = { controls_state = 223 }
					}
					AND = {
						owns_state = 243
						NOT = { controls_state = 243 }
					}
					AND = {
						owns_state = 224
						NOT = { controls_state = 224 }
					}
					AND = {
						owns_state = 222
						NOT = { controls_state = 222 }
					}
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SOV_save_pp_for_manpower_trouble = yes
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					controls_state = 219
				}
				219 = { #Moscow
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 6
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 2
					}
				}
				573 = { #Zlatoust
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 4
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 3
						instant_build = yes
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 0.3 }
						damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 0.1 }
					}
				}
				582 = { #Magnitogorsk
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 4
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 3
						instant_build = yes
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}

					hidden_effect = {
						damage_building = { type = arms_factory damage = 0.3 }
						damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 0.1 }
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = relocate_industry_repair_russia2
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_relocate_industry_from_moscow_tt_russia2
		}
	}

	#202 "Kiev"
	SOV_hold_kiev_russia2 = {

		icon = generic_civil_support

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		#Fail trigger
		available = {
			NOT = { controls_state = 202 }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			state = 202
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 90

		fire_only_once = yes

		is_good = yes

		activation = {
			is_subject = no
			has_government = communism
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Joseph Stalin"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Vasily Stalin"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			has_war = yes
			has_civil_war = no
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_major = yes
				capital_scope = {
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
			}
			surrender_progress > 0
			any_enemy_country = {
				any_state = {
					is_controlled_by = PREV
					distance_to = {
						value < 500
						target = 202
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = second_civil_war_in_progress
				has_country_flag = black_revolution_civil_war_in_progress
			}
			202 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}

		#Success
		timeout_effect = {
			add_war_support = 0.05
			add_political_power = 100
			202 = { save_event_target_as = state_defended_gpw_russia2 }
			country_event = soviets.495
		}
		#Fail
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			202 = { save_event_target_as = state_defended_gpw_russia2 }
			country_event = soviets.496
		}
	}

	#Capture 202 "Berlin"
	SOV_capture_berlin_russia2 = {

		icon = generic_tank

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		#Success trigger
		available = {
			OR = {
				controls_state = 64
				any_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_war_together_with = ROOT
					controls_state = 64
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			state = 64
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 180

		fire_only_once = yes

		is_good = no

		activation = {
			is_subject = no
			has_government = communism
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Joseph Stalin"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Vasily Stalin"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			has_war = yes
			has_civil_war = no
			surrender_progress < 0.05
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_major = yes
				capital_scope = {
					state = 64
				}
			}
			any_state = {
				distance_to = {
					value < 500
					target = 64
				}
				OR = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						controls_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = second_civil_war_in_progress
				has_country_flag = black_revolution_civil_war_in_progress
				controls_state = 64
				owns_state = 64
			}
		}

		#Fail
		timeout_effect = {
			add_war_support = -0.05
			add_political_power = -100
			64 = { save_event_target_as = state_captured_gpw_russia2 }
			country_event = soviets.498
		}
		#Success
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army1
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army1
					add_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army2
					add_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army3
					add_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army4
					add_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army5
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army1
			}
			64 = { save_event_target_as = state_captured_gpw_russia2 }
			country_event = soviets.497
		}
	}

	#Capture 2 "Rome"
	SOV_capture_rome_russia2 = {

		icon = generic_tank

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		#Success trigger
		available = {
			OR = {
				controls_state = 2
				any_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_war_together_with = ROOT
					controls_state = 2
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			state = 2
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 180

		fire_only_once = yes

		is_good = no

		activation = {
			is_subject = no
			has_government = communism
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Joseph Stalin"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Vasily Stalin"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			has_war = yes
			has_civil_war = no
			surrender_progress < 0.05
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_major = yes
				capital_scope = {
					state = 2
				}
			}
			any_state = {
				distance_to = {
					value < 500
					target = 2
				}
				OR = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					any_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						controls_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = second_civil_war_in_progress
				has_country_flag = black_revolution_civil_war_in_progress
				controls_state = 2
				owns_state = 2
			}
		}

		#Fail
		timeout_effect = {
			add_war_support = -0.05
			add_political_power = -100
			2 = { save_event_target_as = state_captured_gpw_russia2 }
			country_event = soviets.498
		}
		#Success
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army1
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army1
					add_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army2
					add_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army3
					add_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army4
					add_idea = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army5
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = SOV_Unstoppable_red_army1
			}
			2 = { save_event_target_as = state_captured_gpw_russia2 }
			country_event = soviets.497
		}
	}

SOV_greater_kurdistan = {

	SOV_ask_kurdistan_territory = {

		icon = GFX_decision_ger_military_buildup

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 10

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		available = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					is_neighbor_of = ROOT
					any_country = {
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
						is_neighbor_of = FROM
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			is_subject = no
			has_government = neutrality
			has_completed_focus = SOV_fate_turkey
			KUR = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
			has_country_flag = choose_kurdistan_over_other
			is_subject = no
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					tag = ROOT
					tag = KUR
				}
				any_state = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = FROM
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = KUR
						is_core_of = KUR
					}
				}
			}
		}

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_fate_turkey
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					tag = ROOT
					tag = KUR
				}
				any_state = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = FROM
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = KUR
						is_core_of = KUR
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		war_with_target_on_remove = yes

		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = soviets.506
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 0.9
				}
			}
		}
	}

	SOV_give_back_kurdistan_territory = {

		icon = GFX_decision_ger_military_buildup

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		state_target = yes

		available = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = {
					is_core_of = KUR
					is_claimed_by = KUR
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			ROOT = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				is_subject = no
				has_government = neutrality
				has_completed_focus = SOV_fate_turkey
				has_country_flag = choose_kurdistan_over_other
				is_subject = no
			}
			KUR = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
			FROM = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = {
					is_core_of = KUR
					is_claimed_by = KUR
				}
			}
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = {
					is_core_of = KUR
					is_claimed_by = KUR
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			KUR = {
				transfer_state = FROM
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

SOV_slavic_help = {

	SOV_help_slavic = {

		icon = GFX_decision_ger_military_buildup

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 30

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		visible = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_completed_focus = SOV_slavic_assistance
			has_government = neutrality
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				has_country_flag = sov_invited_focus_tsar
			}
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = sov_helping_slavic_country
			}
		}

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = SOV_slavic_assistance
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				has_country_flag = sov_invited_focus_tsar
			}
		}

		cost = 25

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = sov_helping_slavic_country
		}

		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = sov_helping_slavic_country
			FROM = {
				country_event = soviets.505
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 80
		}
	}
}

	SOV_gather_support_tsar = {

		icon = hol_radio_oranje

		fire_only_once = yes

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}
		
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = sov_anna_anderson_struggle_over
			}
			has_country_flag = sov_anna_anderson_returns_russia
			has_government = neutrality
			is_subject = no
			has_capitulated = no
			has_completed_focus = SOV_restoration_tsar
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = {

					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Vladimir Kirillovich"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = SOV_the_emperor

					name = "Anastasia Nikolaevna"
					ruling_only = yes
				}

			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = sov_gathering_support_anna

		}

		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = sov_gathering_support_tsar

		}

			custom_modifier_tooltip = anna_anderson_legitimacy_gain_daily_minus_02

						value = 0.5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals

				add_to_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy = 0.03 }
				clamp_variable = {

					max = 1
				}
				set_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = anna_anderson_legitimacy }
				multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 2 }
				round_variable = anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui
				clamp_variable = {
					var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
					min = 0
					max = 200
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = anna_anderson_add_legitimacy_3
			}
			else = {
				subtract_from_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy = 0.03 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
					min = 0
					max = 1
				}
				set_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = anna_anderson_legitimacy }
				multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 100 }
				multiply_variable = { anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui = 2 }
				round_variable = anna_anderson_legitimacy_gui
				clamp_variable = {
					var = anna_anderson_legitimacy
					min = 0
					max = 200
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = anna_anderson_remove_legitimacy_3
			}
		}
	}

			is_subject = no
			has_capitulated = no

					name = "Kirill Vladimirovich"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Vladimir Kirillovich"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = SOV_the_emperor
				has_completed_focus = SOV_the_empress
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Anastasia Nikolaevna"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}

		is_good = no

		fire_only_once = yes

            country_event = soviets.514
        }

SOV_encourage_investments_democratic_decisions = {

	SOV_encourage_investment_democratic_in_state = {

		icon = gre_paying_ifc_debt

		state_target = yes

		target_array = sov_democratic_investments_random_states

		available = {
			FROM = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
			political_power_daily > 0.09
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			owns_state = FROM
			has_government = democratic
			is_subject = no
			has_capitulated = no
			has_completed_focus = SOV_encourage_investments
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 10

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		days_remove = 90

		complete_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { cost_pp_infrastructure = 10 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { cost_pp_infrastructure = FROM.infrastructure_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { cost_pp_infrastructure = -10 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = cost_pp_infrastructure
							value = 0
							compare = equals
						}
					}
				}
				add_political_power = var:cost_pp_infrastructure
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -0.1
		}

		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 4
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_coastal = yes
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

			set_country_flag = sov_democratic_target_alliance

					}
				}
				country_event = soviets.527
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = SOV.current_democratic_vote^0
						value = SOV.current_democratic_vote^1

						any_neighbor_state = {
							is_core_of = GER
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER
						}
					}
					POL = {
						is_subject_of = SOV
						any_state = {
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = PREV
							any_neighbor_state = {
								is_core_of = GER
								is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_exists = GER
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = GER
				GER = {
					OR = {
						is_subject_of = SOV
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = has_successfully_contacted_german_exile_monarch
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
					has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
					has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 100

		days_remove = 70

		cancel_trigger = {
			has_war_with = GER
		}

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							state = 762
						}
						is_core_of = GER
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER
						any_neighbor_state = {
							OR = {
								is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
								is_owned_and_controlled_by = POL
							}
							NOT = {
								has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_1
								has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_2
								has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_3
								has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_4
								has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_5
							}
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = random_prussian_state_1
				}
				GER = {
					activate_mission = SOV_civil_war_monarchy_incomming
					set_country_flag = is_victim_of_russia_civil_war
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = release_imperial_prussia_and_strat_war_with_germany
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = will_launch_monarchist_insurrection
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							state = 762
						}
						is_core_of = GER
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER
						any_neighbor_state = {
							OR = {
								is_owned_and_controlled_by = SOV
								is_owned_and_controlled_by = POL
							}
							NOT = {
								has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_1
								has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_2
								has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_3
							}
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = random_prussian_state_2
				}
				country_event = { id = germanys.34 }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_1
							has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_2
							has_state_flag = random_prussian_state_3
						}
					}
					PRE = {
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
				GER = {
					release = PRE
					clr_country_flag = is_victim_of_russia_civil_war
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = GER
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						POL = {
							is_subject_of = SOV
						}
					}
					POL = {
						add_to_war = { 
							targeted_alliance = SOV 
							enemy = GER
							hostility_reason = asked_to_join
						}
					}
				}
				PRE = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = GEC
					declare_war_on = {
						target = GER
						type = annex_everything
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							SOV = {
								has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
							}

		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_demand

			original_tag = SOV

				has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
				has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
			}
			FROM = {
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = PREV
					is_core_of = GER
				}
				NOT = {
					TAG = GER
					TAG = SOV
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = PREV
					is_core_of = GER
				}
				NOT = {
					TAG = GER
					TAG = SOV
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					is_subject_of = SOV
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = has_successfully_contacted_german_exile_monarch
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
					has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
					has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
				}
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = from_own_core_of_germany
				FROM = {
					any_state = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = PREV
						is_core_of = GER
					}
				} 
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = soviets.229 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 80
		}
	}
