	SOV_restore_bavaria_monarchy = {

		icon = GFX_decision_eng_support_imperialist_coup
	
		fire_only_once = yes

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = decide_to_restore_prussia_and_other_kingdom
			NOT = {
				country_exists = CFR
			}
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = CFR
			}
			has_war = no
			is_subject = no
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = bavaria_is_owned_by_root_or_puppet
				OR = {
					54 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
					any_country = {
						owns_state = 54
						is_subject_of = SOV
					}
				}
				OR = {
					53 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
					any_country = {
						owns_state = 53
						is_subject_of = SOV
					}
				}	
				OR = {
					52 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
					any_country = {
						owns_state = 52
						is_subject_of = SOV
					}
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = release_bavaria_as_puppet
			hidden_effect = {
				BAY = {
					add_state_core = 52
					add_state_core = 53
					add_state_core = 54
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = BAY
						any_country = {
							OR = {
								TAG = SOV
								is_subject_of = SOV
							}	
							owns_state = PREV
						}
					}
					BAY = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = BAY
						autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
					}
				}
				BAY = {
					division_template = {
						name = "Bavarian Division"
						priority = 1
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 4 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 4 }
						}
						support = {
							engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							artillery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"1st Bavarian Division\" division_template = \"Bavarian Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
							owner = BAY
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"2nd Bavarian Division\" division_template = \"Bavarian Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
							owner = BAY
						}
					}
					random_owned_controlled_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"3rd Bavarian Division\" division_template = \"Bavarian Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
							owner = BAY
						}
					}
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 10
						neutrality = 70
						fascism = 10
						communism = 10	
					}
				}
			}
		}

	SOV_fate_of_poland_monarchist_choice_subject = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_operation
	
		fire_only_once = yes

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SOV
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = poland_accept_imperial_puppet
			has_country_flag = restoration_german_monarchy_kaiser
		}

		available = {
			country_exists = POL
			is_subject = no
			has_war = no
			has_government = neutrality
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = decide_to_restore_prussia_and_other_kingdom
					country_exists = PRE
					PRE = {
						is_subject_of = SOV
					}
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SOV_fate_of_poland_monarchist_choice_subject_tt_trig_pre
					PRE = {
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = SOV
							AND = {
								is_in_faction_with = SOV
								has_government = neutrality
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = has_successfully_contacted_german_exile_monarch
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet
						has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_puppet_reduced
						has_country_flag = ger_exiles_accept_no_puppet
					}
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SOV_fate_of_poland_monarchist_choice_subject_tt_trig
					GER = {
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = SOV
							AND = {
								is_in_faction_with = SOV
								has_government = neutrality
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			POL = {
				is_subject_of = SOV
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			country_event = { id = soviets.248 }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 80
		}
	}

					}
					set_state_flag = french_state_before_monarchist_war

			}

			factor = 80
		}

						}
					}
				}

					var = randomize_french_monarchist_leader_influence_var
					distribution = uniform
					min = 0
					max = 100
				}
				round_variable = randomize_french_monarchist_leader_influence_var
				add_to_variable = {
					var = french_monarchist_leader_influence_var
			    	value = randomize_french_monarchist_leader_influence_var
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							var = french_monarchist_leader_influence_var
							value = 100
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
					SOV = {
						set_autonomy = {
							target = FRA
							autonomy_state = autonomy_imperial_governorates
						}
					}
					FRA = {
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 10
							neutrality = 70
							fascism = 10
							communism = 10
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					SOV = {
						add_to_faction = FRA
					}
					FRA = {
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = alliance
							id = SOV
							value = 100
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 80
		}
	}

UKR_industrial_revival_project = {

	UKR_mass_infrastructure_investment = {

		icon = generic_construction

		allowed = {
			original_tag = UKR
		}

		visible = {
			any_state = {
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
				infrastructure < 10
			}
		}

		available = {
			surrender_progress < 0.25
		}

		cost = 100

		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					infrastructure < 10
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	UKR_ask_early_factories = {

		icon = generic_factory

		days_re_enable = 25

		allowed = {
			original_tag = UKR
		}

		visible = {
			check_variable = {
				var = ukr_ask_early_factories_count
				value = 5
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
		}

		available = {
			surrender_progress < 0.25
		}

		cost = 15

		complete_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					infrastructure < 10
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = UKR_Early_payments
					}
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = UKR_Early_payments
					days = 50
				}
			}
			else = {
				modify_timed_idea = {
					idea = UKR_Early_payments
					days = 50
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { ukr_ask_early_factories_count = 1 }
		}
	}

	UKR_ask_early_guns = {

		icon = generic_industry

					}

				}

				}
				check_variable = {
					var = pay_in_advance_three
					value = 2
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = has_idea_industrial_revival_tt
				OR = {
					has_idea = UKR_Industrial_revival
					has_idea = UKR_Industrial_revival2
					has_idea = UKR_Industrial_revival3
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 25

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = UKR_Industrial_revival
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { ukr_days_remove_phase_one = 50 }
				add_to_variable = { pay_in_advance_one = 1 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = phase_one_loses_50_days
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = UKR_Industrial_revival2
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { ukr_days_remove_phase_two = 50 }
				add_to_variable = { pay_in_advance_two = 1 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = phase_two_loses_50_days
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = UKR_Industrial_revival3
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { ukr_days_remove_phase_three = 50 }
				add_to_variable = { pay_in_advance_three = 1 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = phase_three_loses_50_days
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = UKR_Early_payments
					}
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = UKR_Early_payments
					days = 50
				}
			}
			else = {
				modify_timed_idea = {
					idea = UKR_Early_payments
					days = 50
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

		}

		}

			clr_country_flag = UKR_revival_project_one_started
			set_country_flag = UKR_revival_project_one_finished
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = UKR_Industrial_revival
				add_idea = UKR_Industrial_revival2
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3

					type = industrial_complex
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_coastal = yes
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}

political_actions = {

	UKR_rename_kiev = {

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_decision
		
		allowed = {
			tag = UKR
		}

		visible = {
			owns_state = 202
		}

		highlight_states = {
			state = 202
		}

		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 202
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = UKR_kiev_renamed
				}
				reset_province_name = 525
				hidden_effect = {
					clr_global_flag = UKR_kiev_renamed
					202 = {
						reset_state_name = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_province_name = { id = 525 name = "Kyiv" }
				hidden_effect = {
					set_global_flag = UKR_kiev_renamed
					202 = {
						set_state_name = "Kyiv"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
